+@app.route('/api/treatments', methods=['GET'])
+def get_treatments():
+    """Get treatment information from the database. Supports ?crop=Maize&disease=Common Rust"""
+    import sqlite3
+    crop = request.args.get('crop', '')
+    disease = request.args.get('disease', '')
+    
+    db_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))), 'database', 'crop_disease.db')
+    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
+    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
+    cursor = conn.cursor()
+    
+    if crop and disease:
+        cursor.execute("SELECT * FROM treatments WHERE LOWER(crop)=LOWER(?) AND LOWER(disease) LIKE LOWER(?)", (crop, f'%{disease}%'))
+    elif crop:
+        cursor.execute("SELECT * FROM treatments WHERE LOWER(crop)=LOWER(?)", (crop,))
+    else:
+        cursor.execute("SELECT * FROM treatments")
+    
+    rows = cursor.fetchall()
+    result = []
+    for row in rows:
+        import json
+        advanced = None
+        if "advanced_treatments" in row.keys() and row["advanced_treatments"]:
+            advanced = json.loads(row["advanced_treatments"])
+            
+        result.append({
+            "id": row["id"],
+            "crop": row["crop"],
+            "disease": row["disease"],
+            "description": row["description"],
+            "symptoms": row["symptoms"],
+            "cause": row["cause"],
+            "treatment": row["treatment"],
+            "prevention": row["prevention"],
+            "do_list": row["do_list"].split("|"),
+            "dont_list": row["dont_list"].split("|"),
+            "advanced": advanced
+        })
+    conn.close()
+    return jsonify({"success": True, "treatments": result})

+
+        async function fetchTreatmentFromDB() {
+            const detailDiv = document.getElementById('dbTreatmentDetail');
+            const disName = document.getElementById('disName')?.textContent || '';
+
+            // Determine crop from disease name
+            let crop = lastScanCrop;
+            if (!crop) {
+                const disLower = disName.toLowerCase();
+                if (disLower.includes('maize') || disLower.includes('corn') || disLower.includes('rust') && disLower.includes('common')) crop = 'Maize';
+                else if (disLower.includes('wheat') || disLower.includes('stripe') || disLower.includes('brown rust') || disLower.includes('septoria')) crop = 'Wheat';
+                else if (disLower.includes('tomato') || disLower.includes('blight') || disLower.includes('leaf mould') || disLower.includes('bacterial')) crop = 'Tomato';
+                else crop = 'Maize'; // default
+            }
+
+            let disease = lastScanDisease || disName;
+            // Clean up disease name for DB query
+            disease = disease.replace(/^(Maize|Wheat|Tomato)\s*[-_]\s*/i, '').trim();
+
+            detailDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
+            document.getElementById('dbDiseaseName').textContent = 'Loading...';
+
+            try {
+                const res = await fetch(`/api/treatments?crop=${encodeURIComponent(crop)}&disease=${encodeURIComponent(disease)}`);
+                const data = await res.json();
+
+                if (data.success && data.treatments.length > 0) {
+                    const t = data.treatments[0];
+                    document.getElementById('dbDiseaseName').textContent = `${t.crop} - ${t.disease}`;
+                    document.getElementById('dbDesc').textContent = t.description;
+                    document.getElementById('dbSymptoms').textContent = t.symptoms;
+                    document.getElementById('dbCause').textContent = t.cause;
+                    document.getElementById('dbTreatment').textContent = t.treatment;
+                    document.getElementById('dbPrevention').textContent = t.prevention;
+
+                    const doList = document.getElementById('dbDoList');
+                    const dontList = document.getElementById('dbDontList');
+                    doList.innerHTML = '';
+                    dontList.innerHTML = '';
+
+                    t.do_list.forEach(item => {
+                        const li = document.createElement('li');
+                        li.textContent = item;
+                        doList.appendChild(li);
+                    });
+                    t.dont_list.forEach(item => {
+                        const li = document.createElement('li');
+                        li.textContent = item;
+                        dontList.appendChild(li);
+                    });
+
+                    detailDiv.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
+                } else {
+                    document.getElementById('dbDiseaseName').textContent = 'No treatment data found';
+                    document.getElementById('dbDesc').textContent = `No matching treatment record found in the database for "${crop} - ${disease}". The database contains treatments for common diseases of Maize, Wheat, and Tomato.`;
+                }
+            } catch (e) {
+                console.error('Treatment DB fetch error:', e);
+                document.getElementById('dbDiseaseName').textContent = 'Error loading treatment data';
+                document.getElementById('dbDesc').textContent = 'Could not connect to the treatment database.';
+            }
+        }

+                        <span class="text-[10px] text-green-500 font-bold flex items-center gap-1">
+                            <span class="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-green-500 animate-pulse"></span> Online
+                        </span>
+                    </div>
+                </div>
+                <button onclick="closeAiDrawer()"
+                    class="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl hover:bg-slate-100 dark:hover:bg-slate-800 flex items-center justify-center transition-all">
+                    <i class="fas fa-times opacity-50"></i>
+                </button>
+            </div>
+
+            <div id="aiContextBadge" class="ai-context-badge">
+                <i class="fas fa-microscope"></i>
+                <span id="aiContextText">Scan data loaded</span>
+            </div>
+
+            <div id="aiDrawerMessages" class="ai-drawer-messages">
+                <!-- Messages get injected here -->
+            </div>
+
+            <div class="ai-drawer-input">
+                <input type="text" id="aiDrawerInput" placeholder="Ask about your results..."
+                    onkeypress="if(event.key === 'Enter') sendAiDrawerMessage()">
+                <button onclick="sendAiDrawerMessage()">
+                    <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i>
+                </button>
+            </div>
+        </div>
+    </div>
+
+    <script>
+        // ===== ASK AI DRAWER LOGIC =====
+        function getAiScanContext() {
+            const res = window.lastScanResult;
+            if (!res) return null;
+
+            // Get remedies and precautions from the REMEDIES_DATA
+            const h = res.health_status === 'healthy';
+            const diseaseKey = h ? 'healthy' : (res.disease_name || 'unhealthy');
+            const activeData = REMEDIES_DATA[diseaseKey] || REMEDIES_DATA['unhealthy'];
+
+            return {
+                crop_type: res.crop_type,
+                health_status: res.health_status,
+                disease_name: res.disease_name || 'None',
+                confidence: `${(res.confidence * 100).toFixed(1)}%`,
+                remedies: activeData.rem || [],
+                precautions: activeData.pre || []
+            };
+        }
+
+        function openAiDrawer() {
+            const overlay = document.getElementById('aiDrawerOverlay');
+            const messages = document.getElementById('aiDrawerMessages');
+            const contextBadge = document.getElementById('aiContextText');
+
+            // Build context badge text
+            const ctx = getAiScanContext();
+            if (ctx) {
+                const statusEmoji = ctx.health_status === 'healthy' ? '✅' : '⚠️';
+                contextBadge.textContent = `${statusEmoji} ${ctx.crop_type.toUpperCase()} • ${ctx.health_status === 'healthy' ? 'Healthy' : ctx.disease_name} • ${ctx.confidence}`;
+            }
+
+            // Reset messages with greeting
+            messages.innerHTML = '';
+            const greeting = document.createElement('div');
+            greeting.className = 'ai-msg bot';
+            greeting.innerHTML = `<b>Hi! I've analyzed your scan results.</b><br><br>` +
+                (ctx ?
+                    `Your <b>${ctx.crop_type}</b> was detected as <b>${ctx.health_status === 'healthy' ? 'Healthy ✅' : ctx.disease_name + ' ⚠️'}</b> with <b>${ctx.confidence}</b> confidence.<br><br>Ask me anything ” treatment plans, causes, prevention, or next steps!` :
+                    `I don't see any scan data yet. Please analyze an image first!`);
+            messages.appendChild(greeting);
+
+            // Show drawer
+            overlay.classList.add('open');
+            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
+
+            // Focus input
+            setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('aiDrawerInput').focus(), 400);
+        }
+
+        function closeAiDrawer(event) {
+            if (event && event.target !== event.currentTarget) return;
+            const overlay = document.getElementById('aiDrawerOverlay');
+            overlay.classList.remove('open');
+            document.body.style.overflow = '';
+        }
+
+        async function sendAiDrawerMessage() {
+            const input = document.getElementById('aiDrawerInput');
+            const msg = input.value.trim();
+            if (!msg) return;
+
+            const messages = document.getElementById('aiDrawerMessages');
+            input.value = '';
+
+            // Add user message
+            const userDiv = document.createElement('div');
+            userDiv.className = 'ai-msg user';
+            userDiv.textContent = msg;
+            messages.appendChild(userDiv);
+
+            // Add typing indicator
+            const typingDiv = document.createElement('div');
+            typingDiv.className = 'ai-typing-indicator';
+            typingDiv.id = 'aiTyping';
+            typingDiv.innerHTML = '<span></span><span></span><span></span>';
+            messages.appendChild(typingDiv);
+            messages.scrollTop = messages.scrollHeight;
+
+            // Build payload with full context
+            const ctx = getAiScanContext();
+            const payload = { message: msg };
+            if (ctx) payload.context = ctx;
+
+            try {
+                const res = await fetch('/api/chat', {
+                    method: 'POST',
+                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
+                    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
+                }).then(r => r.json());
+
+                // Remove typing indicator
+                const typing = document.getElementById('aiTyping');
+                if (typing) typing.remove();
+
+                // Add bot response
+                const botDiv = document.createElement('div');
+                botDiv.className = 'ai-msg bot';
+                if (res.error) {
+                    botDiv.innerHTML = `<span style="color: #EF4444;">${res.error}</span>`;
+                } else {
+                    // Format response: bold, line breaks
+                    let formatted = res.response
+                        .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<b>$1</b>')
+                        .replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
+                    botDiv.innerHTML = formatted;
+                }
+                messages.appendChild(botDiv);
+            } catch (e) {
+                const typing = document.getElementById('aiTyping');
+                if (typing) typing.remove();
+
+                const errDiv = document.createElement('div');
+                errDiv.className = 'ai-msg bot';
+                errDiv.innerHTML = '<span style="color: #EF4444;">Connection failed. Please try again.</span>';
+                messages.appendChild(errDiv);
+            }
+
+            messages.scrollTop = messages.scrollHeight;
+        }
+    </script>
+
+
+<script>
+    // ===== TREATMENT DATABASE LOGIC =====
+    function showTreatCrop(crop) {
+        document.getElementById('treatCropSelector').classList.add('hidden');
+        document.getElementById('treatCropDetails').classList.remove('hidden');
+        
+        document.querySelectorAll('.treat-crop-list').forEach(el => el.classList.add('hidden'));
+        const target = document.getElementById('treat-crop-' + crop);
+        if (target) {
+            target.classList.remove('hidden');
+        }
+    }
+
+    function hideTreatCrop() {
+        document.getElementById('treatCropDetails').classList.add('hidden');
+        document.getElementById('treatCropSelector').classList.remove('hidden');
+    }
+
+    function calcCost(e, range) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        const acres = prompt("Enter your farm size in acres to calculate total estimated cost:");
+        if (acres && !isNaN(acres)) {
+            const nums = range.match(/\d+/g);
+            if (nums && nums.length >= 2) {
+                const min = parseInt(nums[0]) * parseFloat(acres);
+                const max = parseInt(nums[1]) * parseFloat(acres);
+                alert(`Estimated Total Cost for ${acres} acres:\n₹${min.toLocaleString()} - ₹${max.toLocaleString()}`);
+            } else {
+                alert("Could not parse cost range.");
+            }
+        }
+    }
+</script>
+
 </body>
 
 </html>
